The\\n70:  * class {@code ClassLoader} is an abstract class.  Given the <a\\n71:  * href=\\\"#binary-name\\\">binary name</a> of a class, a class loader should attempt to\\n72:  * locate or generate data that constitutes a definition for the class.  A\\n73:  * typical strategy is to transform the name into a file name and then read a\\n74:  * \\\"class file\\\" of that name from a file system.\\n75:  *\\n76:  * <p> Every {@link java.lang.Class Class} object contains a {@link\\n77:  * Class#getClassLoader() reference} to the {@code ClassLoader} that defined\\n78:  * it.\\n79:  *\\n80:  * <p> {@code Class} objects for array classes are not created by class\\n81:  * loaders, but are created automatically as required by the Java runtime.\\n82:  * The class loader for an array class, as returned by {@link\\n83:  * Class#getClassLoader()} is the same as the class loader for its element\\n84:  * type; if the element type is a primitive type, then the array class has no\\n85:  * class loader.\\n86:  *\\n87:  * <p> Applications implement subclasses of {@code ClassLoader} in order to\\n88:  * extend the manner in which the Java virtual machine dynamically loads\\n89:  * classes.\\n90:  *\\n91:  * <p> In addition to loading classes, a class loader is also responsible for\\n92:  * locating resources. A resource is some data (a \\\"{@code .class}\\\" file,\\n93:  * configuration data, or an image for example) that is identified with an\\n94:  * abstract '/'-separated path name. Resources are typically packaged with an\\n95:  * application or library so that they can be located by code in the\\n96:  * application or library. In some cases, the resources are included so that\\n97:  * they can be located by other libraries.\\n98:  *\\n99:  * <p> The {@code ClassLoader} class uses a delegation model to search for\\n100:  * classes and resources.  Each instance of {@code ClassLoader} has an\\n101:  * associated parent class loader. When requested to find a class or\\n102:  * resource, a {@code ClassLoader} instance will usually delegate the search\\n103:  * for the class or resource to its parent class loader before attempting to\\n104:  * find the class or resource itself.\\n105:  *\\n106:  * <p> Class loaders that support concurrent loading of classes are known as\\n107:  * <em>{@linkplain #isRegisteredAsParallelCapable() parallel capable}</em> class\\n108:  * loaders and are required to register themselves at their class initialization\\n109:  * time by invoking the {@link\\n110:  * #registerAsParallelCapable ClassLoader.registerAsParallelCapable}\\n111:  * method. Note that the {@code ClassLoader} class is registered as parallel\\n112:  * capable by default. However, its subclasses still need to register themselves\\n113:  * if they are parallel capable.\\n114:  * In environments in which the delegation model is not strictly\\n115:  * hierarchical, class loaders need to be parallel capable, otherwise class\\n116:  * loading can lead to deadlocks because the loader lock is held for the\\n117:  * duration of the class loading process (see {@link #loadClass\\n118:  * loadClass} methods).\\n119:  *\\n120:  * <h2> <a id=\\\"builtinLoaders\\\">Run-time Built-in Class Loaders</a></h2>\\n121:  *\\n122:  * The Java run-time has the following built-in class loaders:\\n123:  *\\n124:  * <ul>\\n125:  * <li><p>Bootstrap class loader.\\n126:  *     It is the virtual machine's built-in class loader, typically represented\\n127:  *     as {@code null}, and does not have a parent.</li>\\n128:  * <li><p>{@linkplain #getPlatformClassLoader() Platform class loader}.\\n129:  *     The platform class loader is responsible for loading the\\n130:  *     <em>platform classes</em>. All rights reserved.\\n3:  * DO NOT ALTER OR REMOVE COPYRIGHT NOTICES OR THIS FILE HEADER.\\n4:  *\\n5:  * This code is free software; you can redistribute it and/or modify it\\n6:  * under the terms of the GNU General Public License version 2 only, as\\n7:  * published by the Free Software Foundation.\\n8:  *\\n9:  * This code is distributed in the hope that it will be useful, but WITHOUT\\n10:  * ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of MERCHANTABILITY or\\n11:  * FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the GNU General Public License\\n12:  * version 2 for more details (a copy is included in the LICENSE file that\\n13:  * accompanied this code).\\n14:  *\\n15:  * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License version\\n16:  * 2 along with this work; if not, write to the Free Software Foundation,\\n17:  * Inc., 51 Franklin St, Fifth Floor, Boston, MA 02110-1301 USA.\\n18:  *\\n19:  * Please contact Oracle, 500 Oracle Parkway, Redwood Shores, CA 94065 USA\\n20:  * or visit www.oracle.com if you need additional information or have any\\n21:  * questions.\\n22:  *\\n23:  */\\n24: \\n25: #ifndef SHARE_CLASSFILE_SYSTEMDICTIONARY_HPP\\n26: #define SHARE_CLASSFILE_SYSTEMDICTIONARY_HPP\\n27: \\n28: #include \\\"oops/oopHandle.hpp\\\"\\n29: #include \\\"runtime/handles.hpp\\\"\\n30: #include \\\"runtime/signature.hpp\\\"\\n31: #include \\\"utilities/vmEnums.hpp\\\"\\n32: \\n33: // The dictionary in each ClassLoaderData stores all loaded classes, either\\n34: // initiatied by its class loader or defined by its class loader:\\n35: //\\n36: //   class loader -> ClassLoaderData -> Loaded and initiated loaded classes\\n37: //\\n38: // Classes are loaded lazily. The default VM class loader is\\n39: // represented as null.\\n40: \\n41: // The underlying data structure is a concurrent hash table (Dictionary) per\\n42: // ClassLoaderData with a fixed number of buckets. During loading the\\n43: // class loader object is locked, (for the VM loader a private lock object is used).\\n44: // The global SystemDictionary_lock is held for all additions into the ClassLoaderData\\n45: // dictionaries.  TODO: fix lock granularity so that class loading can\\n46: // be done concurrently, but only by different loaders.\\n47: //\\n48: // During loading a placeholder (name, loader) is temporarily placed in\\n49: // a side data structure, and is used to detect ClassCircularityErrors.\\n50: //\\n51: // When class loading is finished, a new entry is added to the dictionary\\n52: // of the class loader and the placeholder is removed.\\n53: //\\n54: // Clients of this class who are interested in finding if a class has\\n55: // been completely loaded -- not classes in the process of being loaded --\\n56: // can read the dictionary unlocked. This is safe because\\n57: //    - entries are only deleted when the class loader is not alive, when the\\n58: //      entire dictionary is deleted.\\n59: //    - entries must be fully formed before they are available to concurrent\\n60: //         readers (we must ensure write ordering)\\n61: //\\n62: // Note that placeholders are deleted at any time, as they are removed\\n63: // when a class is completely loaded. Therefore, readers as well as writers\\n64: // of placeholders must hold the SystemDictionary_lock.\\n65: //\\n66: \\n67: class BootstrapInfo;\\n68: class ClassFileStream;\\n69: class ClassLoadInfo;\\n70: class Dictionary;\\n71: class PackageEntry;\\n72: class GCTimer;\\n73: class EventClassLoad;\\n74: class Symbol;\\n75: \\n76: template <class E> class GrowableArray;\\n77: \\n78: class SystemDictionary : AllStatic {\\n79:   friend class AOTLinkedClassBulkLoader;\\n80:   friend class BootstrapInfo;\\n81:   friend class vmClasses;\\n82:   friend class VMStructs;\\n83: \\n84:  public:\\n85: \\n86:   // Returns a class with a given class name and class loader. The method:\n   - First checks if the class is already loaded via findLoadedClass\n   - If not found and parent is not null, delegates to parent.loadClass()\n   - If parent is null, calls findBootstrapClassOrNull()\n   - If still not found, calls findClass() to load the class\n   - Lines 534-570 contain the implementation\n\n2. **BuiltinClassLoader.java** (`src/java.base/share/classes/jdk/internal/loader/BuiltinClassLoader.java`) - Extends SecureClassLoader and is the base for the three built-in loaders. Implements a modified delegation model for modules.\n\n3. **ClassLoaders.java** (`src/java.base/share/classes/jdk/internal/loader/ClassLoaders.java`) - Creates and manages the three built-in loaders:\n   - BootClassLoader (extends BuiltinClassLoader, parent=null)\n   - PlatformClassLoader (extends BuiltinClassLoader, parent=BootClassLoader)\n   - AppClassLoader (extends BuiltinClassLoader, parent=PlatformClassLoader)\n   The initialization happens in the static block at lines 62-99\n\n4. **BootLoader.java** (`src/java.base/share/classes/jdk/internal/loader/BootLoader.java`) - A utility class for the boot class loader that manages resources and modules\n\n5. **classLoader.cpp** (`src/hotspot/share/classfile/classLoader.cpp`) - The HotSpot C++ implementation for class loading, includes native methods and class loading operations. Includes SystemDictionary for caching.\n   \n6. **systemDictionary.hpp/cpp** (`src/hotspot/share/classfile/systemDictionary.hpp` and `.cpp`) - The C++ layer that maintains a cache of loaded classes through methods like resolve_or_fail(), resolve_or_null(), resolve_from_stream(), and find_instance_klass() for lookups. The delegation chain starts when application code calls ClassLoader.loadClass(), which delegates upward to parent loaders—bootstrap handles core classes, platform delegates to bootstrap then loads platform classes, and application delegates to platform then loads application classes. Core Java API Layer (java.lang.ClassLoader)\\nFile: `src/java.base/share/classes/java/lang/ClassLoader.java`\\n\\nThe `loadClass(String, boolean)` method (lines 534-570) implements the fundamental parent-first delegation model:\\n- First checks if a class is already loaded via `findLoadedClass()`\\n- If not cached and parent exists, delegates to `parent.loadClass()`\\n- If no parent (at bootstrap), calls `findBootstrapClassOrNull()` to check bootstrap classes\\n- If still not found, invokes `findClass()` to load the class\\n- Optionally resolves the class if the `resolve` parameter is true\\n- Uses `getClassLoadingLock()` for thread-safe loading\\n\\n### 2. Built-in ClassLoader Infrastructure (jdk.internal.loader)\\n\\n#### BuiltinClassLoader\\nFile: `src/java.base/share/classes/jdk/internal/loader/BuiltinClassLoader.java`\\n\\nExtends `SecureClassLoader` and forms the base for all three built-in loaders. Key features:\\n- Implements a module-aware delegation model that allows platform loader to delegate to app loader\\n- Manages module loading via `loadModule()` method\\n- Supports loading from URL class paths\\n- Maintains a map of package names to loaded modules\\n- Registered as parallel capable for concurrent class loading\\n\\n#### ClassLoaders Factory\\nFile: `src/java.base/share/classes/jdk/internal/loader/ClassLoaders.java`\\n\\nCreates and manages the three built-in loaders (lines 62-99):\\n\\n1. **BootClassLoader** (lines 131-140): \\n   - Parent: `null`\\n   - Loads core JDK classes from bootstrap classpath\\n   - Extends BuiltinClassLoader\\n\\n2. **PlatformClassLoader** (lines 146-155):\\n   - Parent: BootClassLoader\\n   - Loads Java SE platform APIs and JDK implementation classes\\n   - Extends BuiltinClassLoader\\n\\n3. **AppClassLoader** (lines 161-187):\\n   - Parent: PlatformClassLoader\\n   - Loads user application classes from the application classpath\\n   - Extends BuiltinClassLoader\\n   - Supports dynamic instrumentation via `appendToClassPathForInstrumentation()`\\n\\n#### BootLoader Utility\\nFile: `src/java.base/share/classes/jdk/internal/loader/BootLoader.java`\\n\\nProvides a restricted API for accessing the boot class loader's unnamed module and service catalog. Manages native libraries and module resources for the boot loader.\\n\\n### 3. HotSpot Native Implementation\\n\\n#### Class Loading Engine\\nFile: `src/hotspot/share/classfile/classLoader.cpp`\\n\\nImplements native class loading operations in C++:\\n- Handles bootstrap classpath parsing and initialization\\n- Loads classes using the jimage file format or exploded JDK directories\\n- Manages JAR file caching and resource loading\\n- Integrates with the SystemDictionary for caching loaded classes\\n\\n#### SystemDictionary Class Cache\\nFile: `src/hotspot/share/classfile/systemDictionary.hpp` and `systemDictionary.cpp`\\n\\nThe C++ `SystemDictionary` class (line 78 in .hpp) is the central repository for all loaded classes in the VM:\\n- Maintains a concurrent hash table dictionary per ClassLoaderData\\n- Stores loaded and initiated classes by class name and loader\\n- Provides key methods:\\n  - `resolve_or_fail()`: Loads a class or throws exception\\n  - `resolve_or_null()`: Loads a class or returns null\\n  - `resolve_from_stream()`: Loads a class from a byte stream\\n  - `resolve_super_or_fail()`: Resolves superclass with circularity detection\\n  - `find_instance_klass()`: Looks up an already-loaded class\\n- Uses SystemDictionary_lock for synchronization\\n- In systemDictionary.cpp, `compute_java_loaders()` (line 135) initializes the Java-level system and platform loaders\\n- Stores references to `java_system_loader()` and `java_platform_loader()` as OopHandles\\n\\n### Delegation Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Application Code**: Calls `ClassLoader.loadClass(\\\"com.example.MyClass\\\")`\\n2. **AppClassLoader**: Inherits delegation from ClassLoader.loadClass()\\n   - Checks cache via findLoadedClass()\\n   - Delegates to PlatformClassLoader.loadClass()\\n3. **PlatformClassLoader**: Delegates to BootClassLoader.loadClass()\\n4. **BootClassLoader**: Has null parent, calls findBootstrapClassOrNull()\\n5. **HotSpot Layer**: If not found, class loading continues in native code\\n6. **SystemDictionary**: VM caches the loaded Klass object for future lookups\\n7. **Return**: Class object returned up the chain to application code\\n\\nThis hierarchical, parent-first delegation ensures that core classes are always loaded by the bootstrap loader, preventing conflicts and maintaining security boundaries between different trust domains.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
